<s> a rustic seat encircles it <\s>

<s> close to the wall there is a swing <\s>
<s> the sky is clear and sunny <\s>

<s> the action passes throughout midsummer day on the lawn of colonel hope's house near the thames above oxford <\s>
<s> act i the time is morning and the scene a level lawn beyond which the river is running amongst fields <\s>
<s> a huge old beech tree overshadows everything in the darkness of whose hollow many things are hidden <\s>
<s> a rustic seat encircles it <\s>
<s> a low wall clothed in creepers with two openings divides this lawn from the flowery approaches to the house <\s>
<s> close to the wall there is a swing <\s>
<s> the sky is clear and sunny <\s>
<s> colonel hope is seated in a garden chair reading a newspaper through pince nez <\s>
<s> he is fifty five and bald with drooping grey moustaches and a weather darkened face <\s>
<s> he wears a flannel suit and a hat from panama a tennis racquet leans against his chair <\s>
<s> hope comes quickly through the opening of the wall with roses in her hands <\s>
<s> she is going grey she wears tan gauntlets and no hat <\s>
<s> her manner is decided her voice emphatic as though aware that there is no nonsense in its owner's composition <\s>
<s> screened from sight miss beech is seated behind the hollow tree and joy is perched on a lower branch hidden by foliage <\s>
